I came here because of the hotel's reputation, excellent location, and complete facilities. I was not disappointed. As soon as you enter the lobby, you can experience the luxurious a**osphere of the hotel layout. The bath center, restaurant, and bistro are fully equipped. The girls at the front desk were also smart and enthusiastic. They upgraded the rooms for free, and took the initiative to introduce related services (bath center, catering) and guide the location of the elevator. The size of my upgraded twin room is a bit beyond imagination. It not only has two 1.5m wide beds, but also a tatami bed and many other facilities - anyway, it has everything you can think of. It is not only spacious but also Bright, the reason for the brightness is that there are exterior windows in the west and south directions.
There are also shortcomings. Firstly, the interior decoration is a bit old and outdated. Secondly, the position of the light switch and socket at the head of the bed does not match the two large beds, making it awkward and inconvenient to use. In addition, there are too few live broadcast channels on the TV, and the viewing effect is not very good, which makes the supporting services of this star hotel inferior.
